(510-740)===\ndef fp8_quant_dequant(\n    value: torch.Tensor,\n    *,\n    group_size: int = 64,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Simulate checkpoint QAT: power-of-two per-group FP8 then BF16 dequant.\"\"\"\n\n    if value.shape[-1] % group_size:\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"last dimension {value.shape[-1]} must be divisible by group_size {group_size}\"\n        )\n    if value.dtype != torch.bfloat16:\n        raise TypeError(f\"FP8 QAT simulation requires BF16 input, got {value.dtype}\")\n    grouped = value.float().reshape(*value.shape[:-1], -1, group_size)\n    absolute_max = grouped.abs().amax(dim=-1, keepdim=True).clamp_min(1e-4)\n    scale = torch.exp2(torch.ceil(torch.log2(absolute_max / 448.0)))\n    quantized = (grouped / scale).clamp(-448.0, 448.0).to(torch.float8_e4m3fn)\n    return (quantized.float() * scale).reshape_as(value).to(value.dtype)\n\n\ndef window_topk_indices(\n    *,\n    batch_size: int,\n    seqlen: int,\n    start_pos: int,\n    device: torch.device,\n    window_size: int = WINDOW_SIZE,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    if batch_size <= 0 or seqlen <= 0 or start_pos < 0:\n        raise ValueError(\"batch_size/seqlen must be positive and start_pos nonnegative\")\n    if start_pos > 0 and seqlen != 1:\n        raise ValueError(\"incremental window indices require seqlen=1\")\n    if start_pos >= window_size - 1:\n        ring = start_pos % window_size\n        row = torch.cat(\n            (\n                torch.arange(ring + 1, window_size, device=device),\n                torch.arange(0, ring + 1, device=device),\n            )\n        )\n        matrix = row.view(1, 1, -1).expand(batch_size, 1, -1)\n    elif start_pos > 0:\n        row = F.pad(\n            torch.arange(start_pos + 1, device=device),\n            (0, window_size - start_pos - 1),\n            value=-1,\n        )\n        matrix = row.view(1, 1, -1).expand(batch_size, 1, -1)\n    else:\n        base = torch.arange(seqlen, device=device).unsqueeze(1)\n        columns = torch.arange(min(seqlen, window_size), device=device)\n        matrix = (base - window_size + 1).clamp(0) + columns\n        matrix = torch.where(matrix > base, -1, matrix)\n        matrix = matrix.unsqueeze(0).expand(batch_size, -1, -1)\n    return matrix.to(torch.int32).contiguous()\n\n\ndef compressed_topk_indices(\n    *,\n    batch_size: int,\n    seqlen: int,\n    start_pos: int,\n    offset: int,\n    device: torch.device,\n    ratio: int = COMPRESS_RATIO,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    if batch_size <= 0 or seqlen <= 0 or start_pos < 0 or offset < 0:\n        raise ValueError(\"invalid compressed-index dimensions\")\n    if start_pos > 0:\n        if seqlen != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"incremental compressed indices require seqlen=1\")\n        row = torch.arange((start_pos + 1) // ratio, device=device) + offset\n        matrix = row.view(1, 1, -1).expand(batch_size, 1, -1)\n    else:\n        count = seqlen // ratio\n        matrix = torch.arange(count, device=device).repeat(seqlen, 1)\n        visible = torch.arange(1, seqlen + 1, device=device).unsqueeze(1) // ratio\n        matrix = torch.where(matrix >= visible, -1, matrix + offset)\n        matrix = matrix.unsqueeze(0).expand(batch_size, -1, -1)\n    return matrix.to(torch.int32).contiguous()\n\n\ndef torch_sparse_attention(\n    query: torch.Tensor,\n    latent_kv: torch.Tensor,\n    attn_sink: torch.Tensor,\n    topk_indices: torch.Tensor,\n    softmax_scale: float,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Small-shape reference sparse MLA without materializing a full context score.\"\"\"\n\n    if query.ndim != 4 or latent_kv.ndim != 3 or topk_indices.ndim != 3:\n        raise ValueError(\"query/latent_kv/topk_indices must have ranks 4/3/3\")\n    batch, seqlen, heads, head_dim = query.shape\n    if latent_kv.shape[0] != batch or latent_kv.shape[2] != head_dim:\n        raise ValueError(\"query and latent KV shapes are incompatible\")\n    if tuple(topk_indices.shape[:2]) != (batch, seqlen):\n        raise ValueError(\"top-k batch/sequence shape mismatch\")\n    if tuple(attn_sink.shape) != (heads,):\n        raise ValueError(f\"attn_sink shape {tuple(attn_sink.shape)} != ({heads},)\")\n    if query.device != latent_kv.device or query.device != topk_indices.device:\n        raise ValueError(\"attention tensors must share one device\")\n\n    valid = topk_indices >= 0\n    if bool((topk_indices[valid] >= latent_kv.shape[1]).any().item()):\n        raise ValueError(\"top-k index exceeds latent KV capacity\")\n    safe = topk_indices.clamp_min(0).long()\n    batch_index = (\n        torch.arange(batch, device=query.device)\n        .view(batch, 1, 1)\n        .expand_as(safe)\n    )\n    selected = latent_kv[batch_index, safe]\n    scores = torch.einsum(\n        \"bshd,bskd->bshk\", query.float(), selected.float()\n    ) * float(softmax_scale)\n    scores = scores.masked_fill(~valid.unsqueeze(2), float(\"-inf\"))\n    sink = attn_sink.float().view(1, 1, heads, 1)\n    maximum = torch.maximum(scores.amax(dim=-1, keepdim=True), sink)\n    exponent = torch.exp(scores - maximum).masked_fill(~valid.unsqueeze(2), 0.0)\n    denominator = exponent.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True) + torch.exp(sink - maximum)\n    probabilities = exponent / denominator\n    output = torch.einsum(\"bshk,bskd->bshd\", probabilities, selected.float())\n    return output.to(query.dtype)\n\n\ndef _torch_sparse_decode_prevalidated(\n    query: torch.Tensor,\n    latent_kv: torch.Tensor,\n    attn_sink: torch.Tensor,\n    plan: Ratio128DecodePlan,\n    softmax_scale: float,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Fixed-index sparse MLA used after decode-plan validation.\"\"\"\n\n    selected = latent_kv[plan.batch_indices, plan.gather_indices]\n    scores = torch.einsum(\n        \"bshd,bskd->bshk\", query.float(), selected.float()\n    ) * softmax_scale\n    sink = attn_sink.float().view(1, 1, query.shape[2], 1)\n    maximum = torch.maximum(scores.amax(dim=-1, keepdim=True), sink)\n    exponent = torch.exp(scores - maximum)\n    denominator = exponent.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True) + torch.exp(sink - maximum)\n    probabilities = exponent / denominator\n    output = torch.einsum(\"bshk,bskd->bshd\", probabilities, selected.float())\n    return output.to(query.dtype)\n\n\ndef _torch_sparse_decode_padded_prevalidated(\n    query: torch.Tensor,\n    latent_kv: torch.Tensor,\n    attn_sink: torch.Tensor,\n    plan: Ratio128StatefulDecodePlan,\n    softmax_scale: float,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Fixed-width sparse MLA with an explicit mask for ``-1`` padding.\"\"\"\n\n    selected = latent_kv[plan.batch_indices, plan.gather_indices]\n    selected = selected.masked_fill(~plan.valid_mask.unsqueeze(-1), 0.0)\n    scores = torch.einsum(\n        \"bshd,bskd->bshk\", query.float(), selected.float()\n    ) * softmax_scale\n    valid = plan.valid_mask.unsqueeze(2)\n    scores = scores.masked_fill(~valid, float(\"-inf\"))\n    sink = attn_sink.float().view(1, 1, query.shape[2], 1)\n    maximum = torch.maximum(scores.amax(dim=-1, keepdim=True), sink)\n    exponent = torch.exp(scores - maximum).masked_fill(~valid, 0.0)\n    denominator = exponent.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True) + torch.exp(sink - maximum)\n    probabilities = exponent / denominator\n    output = torch.einsum(\"bshk,bskd->bshd\", probabilities, selected.float())\n    return output.to(query.dtype)\n\n\ndef prepare_attention_weights(\n    weights: ResidentAttentionWeights,\n    *,\n    layer_id: int,\n    rank: int,\n    world_size: int,\n    checkpoint_id: str,\n) -> PreparedAttentionWeights:\n    if (\n        not isinstance(layer_id, int)\n        or isinstance(layer_id, bool)\n        or layer_id not in SUPPORTED_RATIO128_LAYER_IDS\n        or not isinstance(world_size, int)\n        or isinstance(world_size, bool)\n        or world_size != 4\n        or not isinstance(rank, int)\n        or isinstance(rank, bool)\n        or rank not in range(world_size)\n    ):\n        raise ValueError(\n            \"prepared attention identity must be a frozen ratio-128 layer on TP4\"\n        )\n    if (\n        not isinstance(checkpoint_id, str)\n        or len(checkpoint_id) != 64\n        or any(character not in \"0123456789abcdef\" for character in checkpoint_id)\n    ):\n        raise ValueError(\"prepared attention requires a lowercase SHA-256 checkpoint_id\")\n    resident_identity = (\n        weights.layer_id,\n        weights.rank,\n        weights.world_size,\n        weights.checkpoint_id,\n    )\n    requested_identity = (layer_id, rank, world_size, checkpoint_id)\n    resident_identity_well_typed = (\n        isinstance(weights.layer_id, int)\n        and not isinstance(weights.layer_id, bool)\n        and isinstance(weights.rank, int)\n        and not isinstance(weights.rank, bool)\n        and isinstance(weights.world_size, int)\n        and not isinstance(weights.world_size, bool)\n        and isinstance(weights.checkpoint_id, str)\n    )\n    if not resident_identity_well_typed or resident_identity != requested_identity:\n        raise ValueError(\n            \"resident ratio-128 attention identity differs from requested identity: \"\n            f\"resident={resident_identity}, requested={requested_identity}\"\n        )\n    if weights.indexer is not None:\n        raise ValueError(\"ratio-128 attention must not contain indexer weights\")\n\n    def linear(value: Any) -> torch.Tensor:\n        return dequant_fp8_block(value.weight, value.scale).to(torch.bfloat16)\n\n    return PreparedAttentionWeights(\n        attn_sink=weights.attn_sink.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        wq_a=linear(weights.wq_a),\n        q_norm=weights.q_norm.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        wq_b=linear(weights.wq_b),\n        wkv=linear(weights.wkv),\n        kv_norm=weights.kv_norm.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        wo_a=linear(weights.wo_a),\n        wo_b=linear(weights.wo_b),\n compressor_wgate=weights.compressor.wgate.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        compressor_norm=weights.compressor.norm.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        layer_id=layer_id,\n        rank=rank,\n torch.where(matrix >= visible, -1, matrix + offset)\n        matrix = matrix.unsqueeze(0).expand(batch_size, -1, -1)\n    return matrix.to(torch.int32).contiguous()\n\n\ndef torch_sparse_attention(\n    query: torch.Tensor,\n    latent_kv: torch.Tensor,\n    attn_sink: torch.Tensor,\n    topk_indices: torch.Tensor,\n    softmax_scale: float,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Small-shape reference sparse MLA without materializing a full context score.\"\"\"\n\n    if query.ndim != 4 or latent_kv.ndim != 3 or topk_indices.ndim != 3:\n        raise ValueError(\"query/latent_kv/topk_indices must have ranks 4/3/3\")\n    batch, seqlen, heads, head_dim = query.shape\n    if latent_kv.shape[0] != batch or latent_kv.shape[2] != head_dim:\n        raise ValueError(\"query and latent KV shapes are incompatible\")\n    if tuple(topk_indices.shape[:2]) != (batch, seqlen):\n        raise ValueError(\"top-k batch/sequence shape mismatch\")\n    if tuple(attn_sink.shape) != (heads,):\n        raise ValueError(f\"attn_sink shape {tuple(attn_sink.shape)} != ({heads},)\")\n    if query.device != latent_kv.device or query.device != topk_indices.device:\n        raise ValueError(\"attention tensors must share one device\")\n\n    valid = topk_indices >= 0\n    if bool((topk_indices[valid] >= latent_kv.shape[1]).any().item()):\n        raise ValueError(\"top-k index exceeds latent KV capacity\")\n    safe = topk_indices.clamp_min(0).long()\n    batch_index = (\n        torch.arange(batch, device=query.device)\n        .view(batch, 1, 1)\n        .expand_as(safe)\n    )\n    selected = latent_kv[batch_index, safe]\n    scores = torch.einsum(\n        \"bshd,bskd->bshk\", query.float(), selected.float()\n    ) * float(softmax_scale)\n    scores = scores.masked_fill(~valid.unsqueeze(2), float(\"-inf\"))\n    sink = attn_sink.float().view(1, 1, heads, 1)\n    maximum = torch.maximum(scores.amax(dim=-1, keepdim=True), sink)\n    exponent = torch.exp(scores - maximum).masked_fill(~valid.unsqueeze(2), 0.0)\n    denominator = exponent.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True) + torch.exp(sink - maximum)\n    probabilities = exponent / denominator\n    output = torch.einsum(\"bshk,bskd->bshd\", probabilities, selected.float())\n    return output.to(query.dtype)\n\n\ndef _torch_sparse_decode_prevalidated(\n    query: torch.Tensor,\n    latent_kv: torch.Tensor,\n    attn_sink: torch.Tensor,\n    plan: Ratio128DecodePlan,\n    softmax_scale: float,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Fixed-index sparse MLA used after decode-plan validation.\"\"\"\n\n    selected = latent_kv[plan.batch_indices, plan.gather_indices]\n    scores = torch.einsum(\n        \"bshd,bskd->bshk\", query.float(), selected.float()\n    ) * softmax_scale\n    sink = attn_sink.float().view(1, 1, query.shape[2], 1)\n    maximum = torch.maximum(scores.amax(dim=-1, keepdim=True), sink)\n    exponent = torch.exp(scores - maximum)\n    denominator = exponent.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True) + torch.exp(sink - maximum)\n    probabilities = exponent / denominator\n    output = torch.einsum(\"bshk,bskd->bshd\", probabilities, selected.float())\n    return output.to(query.dtype)\n\n\ndef _torch_sparse_decode_padded_prevalidated(\n    query: torch.Tensor,\n    latent_kv: torch.Tensor,\n    attn_sink: torch.Tensor,\n    plan: Ratio128StatefulDecodePlan,\n    softmax_scale: float,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Fixed-width sparse MLA with an explicit mask for ``-1`` padding.\"\"\"\n\n    selected = latent_kv[plan.batch_indices, plan.gather_indices]\n    selected = selected.masked_fill(~plan.valid_mask.unsqueeze(-1), 0.0)\n    scores = torch.einsum(\n        \"bshd,bskd->bshk\", query.float(), selected.float()\n    ) * softmax_scale\n    valid = plan.valid_mask.unsqueeze(2)\n    scores = scores.masked_fill(~valid, float(\"-inf\"))\n    sink = attn_sink.float().view(1, 1, query.shape[2], 1)\n    maximum = torch.maximum(scores.amax(dim=-1, keepdim=True), sink)\n    exponent = torch.exp(scores - maximum).masked_fill(~valid, 0.0)\n    denominator = exponent.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True) + torch.exp(sink - maximum)\n    probabilities = exponent / denominator\n    output = torch.einsum(\"bshk,bskd->bshd\", probabilities, selected.float())\n    return output.to(query.dtype)\n\n\ndef prepare_attention_weights(\n    weights: ResidentAttentionWeights,\n    *,\n    layer_id: int,\n    rank: int,\n    world_size: int,\n    checkpoint_id: str,\n) -> PreparedAttentionWeights:\n    if (\n        not isinstance(layer_id, int)\n        or isinstance(layer_id, bool)\n        or layer_id not in SUPPORTED_RATIO128_LAYER_IDS\n        or not isinstance(world_size, int)\n        or isinstance(world_size, bool)\n        or world_size != 4\n        or not isinstance(rank, int)\n        or isinstance(rank, bool)\n        or rank not in range(world_size)\n    ):\n        raise ValueError(\n            \"prepared attention identity must be a frozen ratio-128 layer on TP4\"\n        )\n    if (\n        not isinstance(checkpoint_id, str)\n        or len(checkpoint_id) != 64\n        or any(character not in \"0123456789abcdef\" for character in checkpoint_id)\n    ):\n        raise ValueError(\"prepared attention requires a lowercase SHA-256 checkpoint_id\")\n    resident_identity = (\n        weights.layer_id,\n        weights.rank,\n        weights.world_size,\n        weights.checkpoint_id,\n    )\n    requested_identity = (layer_id, rank, world_size, checkpoint_id)\n    resident_identity_well_typed = (\n        isinstance(weights.layer_id, int)\n        and not isinstance(weights.layer_id, bool)\n        and isinstance(weights.rank, int)\n        and not isinstance(weights.rank, bool)\n        and isinstance(weights.world_size, int)\n        and not isinstance(weights.world_size, bool)\n        and isinstance(weights.checkpoint_id, str)\n    )\n    if not resident_identity_well_typed or resident_identity != requested_identity:\n        raise ValueError(\n            \"resident ratio-128 attention identity differs from requested identity: \"\n            f\"resident={resident_identity}, requested={requested_identity}\"\n        )\n    if weights.indexer is not None:\n        raise ValueError(\"ratio-128 attention must not contain indexer weights\")\n\n    def linear(value: Any) -> torch.Tensor:\n        return dequant_fp8_block(value.weight, value.scale).to(torch.bfloat16)\n\n    return PreparedAttentionWeights(\n        attn_sink=weights.attn_sink.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        wq_a=linear(weights.wq_a),\n        q_norm=weights.q_norm.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        wq_b=linear(weights.wq_b),\n        wkv=linear(weights.wkv),\n        kv_norm=weights.kv_norm.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        wo_a=linear(weights.wo_a),\n        wo_b=linear(weights.wo_b),\n        compressor_ape=weights.compressor.ape.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        compressor_wkv=weights.compressor.wkv.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        compressor_wgate=weights.compressor.wgate.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        compressor_norm=weights.compressor.norm.float().contiguous().clone(),\n        layer_id=layer_id,\n        rank=rank,\n        world_size=world_size,\n        checkpoint_id=checkpoint_id,\n    )\n\n\nclass For DeepSeek-V4-Pro, a layer residual\nhas shape ``[batch, sequence, 4, 7168]``.  ``hc_pre`` reduces the four residual\nstreams to one hidden state, and ``hc_post`` expands a branch output back to\nfour streams while mixing the previous residual streams.\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom __future__ import annotations\n\nimport math\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass\nfrom typing import Literal\n\nimport torch\nimport torch.nn.functional as F\n\n\nHCBranch = Literal[\"attn\", \"ffn\"]\n\n\n@dataclass(frozen=True)\nclass HyperConnectionParameterNames:\n    \"\"\"Checkpoint keys for one layer's attention or FFN HC transform.\"\"\"\n\n    fn: str\n    scale: str\n    base: str\n\n\ndef layer_hc_parameter_names(\n    layer_id: int, branch: HCBranch\n) -> HyperConnectionParameterNames:\n    \"\"\"Return the unmodified checkpoint keys consumed by :func:`hc_pre`.\"\"\"\n\n    if not isinstance(layer_id, int) or isinstance(layer_id, bool) or layer_id < 0:\n        raise ValueError(\"layer_id must be a non-negative integer\")\n    if branch not in (\"attn\", \"ffn\"):\n        raise ValueError(\"branch must be 'attn' or 'ffn'\")\n    prefix = f\"layers.{layer_id}.hc_{branch}\"\n    return HyperConnectionParameterNames(\n        fn=f\"{prefix}_fn\",\n        scale=f\"{prefix}_scale\",\n        base=f\"{prefix}_base\",\n    )\n\n\ndef _require_floating(name: str, tensor: torch.Tensor) -> None:\n    if not tensor.is_floating_point():\n        raise TypeError(f\"{name} must be floating point, got {tensor.dtype}\")\n\n\ndef _validate_sinkhorn(sinkhorn_iters: int, eps: float) -> None:\n    if (\n        not isinstance(sinkhorn_iters, int)\n        or isinstance(sinkhorn_iters, bool)\n        or sinkhorn_iters < 1\n    ):\n        raise ValueError(\"sinkhorn_iters must be a positive integer\")\n    if not math.isfinite(eps) or eps <= 0:\n        raise ValueError(\"HC epsilon must be finite and positive\")\n\n\ndef _validate_hyperparameters(\n    *, norm_eps: float, sinkhorn_iters: int, hc_eps: float\n) -> None:\n    if not math.isfinite(norm_eps) or norm_eps <= 0:\n        raise ValueError(\"norm_eps must be finite and positive\")\n    _validate_sinkhorn(sinkhorn_iters, hc_eps)\n\n\ndef hc_split_sinkhorn(\n    mixes: torch.Tensor,\n    hc_scale: torch.Tensor,\n    hc_base: torch.Tensor,\n    *,\n    hc_mult: int,\n    sinkhorn_iters: int = 20,\n    eps: float = 1e-6,\n) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Split checkpoint-produced logits into pre, post, and residual mixes.\n\n    ``mixes`` is ``[batch, sequence, (2 + hc_mult) * hc_mult]``.  The first\n    ``hc_mult`` values produce the pre-reduction weights, the next ``hc_mult``\n    values produce the branch post weights, and the remaining values produce a\n    Sinkhorn-normalized ``[input_stream, output_stream]`` residual matrix.\n\n    All outputs are float32.  The result shapes are ``[b, s, hc]``,\n    ``[b, s, hc]``, and ``[b, s, hc, hc]`` respectively.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    if mixes.ndim != 3:\n        raise ValueError(f\"mixes must have shape [b, s, mix], got {tuple(mixes.shape)}\")\n    if (\n        not isinstance(hc_mult, int)\n        or isinstance(hc_mult, bool)\n        or hc_mult < 1\n    ):\n        raise ValueError(\"hc_mult must be a positive integer\")\n    _validate_sinkhorn(sinkhorn_iters, eps)\n    _require_floating(\"mixes\", mixes)\n    _require_floating(\"hc_scale\", hc_scale)\n    _require_floating(\"hc_base\", hc_base)\n\n    mix_features = (2 + hc_mult) * hc_mult\n    if mixes.shape[-1] != mix_features:\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"mixes last dimension {mixes.shape[-1]} != {mix_features} for hc_mult={hc_mult}\"\n        )\n    if tuple(hc_scale.shape) != (3,):\n        raise ValueError(f\"hc_scale shape {tuple(hc_scale.shape)} != (3,)\")\n    if tuple(hc_base.shape) != (mix_features,):\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"hc_base shape {tuple(hc_base.shape)} != ({mix_features},)\"\n        )\n    if mixes.device != hc_scale.device or mixes.device != hc_base.device:\n        raise ValueError(\"mixes, hc_scale, and hc_base must be on the same device\")\n\n    logits = mixes.float()\n    scale = hc_scale.float()\n    base = hc_base.float()\n    pre = torch.sigmoid(\n        logits[..., :hc_mult] * scale[0] + base[:hc_mult]\n    ) + eps\n    post = 2.0 * torch.sigmoid(\n        logits[..., hc_mult : 2 * hc_mult] * scale[1]\n        + base[hc_mult : 2 * hc_mult]\n    )\n    comb = (\n        logits[..., 2 * hc_mult :].reshape(*logits.shape[:-1], hc_mult, hc_mult)\n        * scale[2]\n        + base[2 * hc_mult :].reshape(hc_mult, hc_mult)\n    )\n\n    # Match the checkpoint reference exactly: softmax supplies the first row\n    # normalization, followed by a column normalization, then alternating\n    # row/column normalizations for the remaining iterations.\n    comb = torch.softmax(comb, dim=-1) + eps\n    comb = comb / (comb.sum(dim=-2, keepdim=True) + eps)\n    for _ in range(sinkhorn_iters - 1):\n        comb = comb / (comb.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True) + eps)\n        comb = comb / (comb.sum(dim=-2, keepdim=True) + eps)\n    return pre, post, comb\n\n\ndef hc_pre(\n    residual: torch.Tensor,\n    hc_fn: torch.Tensor,\n    hc_scale: torch.Tensor,\n    hc_base: torch.Tensor,\n    *,\n    norm_eps: float = 1e-6,\n    sinkhorn_iters: int = 20,\n    hc_eps: float = 1e-6,\n) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Reduce HC residual streams and create the matching post-update state.\n\n    Contract for the production checkpoint::\n\n        residual [b, s, 4, 7168]\n        hc_fn   [24, 28672]\n        hc_scale [3]\n        hc_base [24]\n          -> hidden [b, s, 7168]       (same dtype as ``residual``)\n          -> post   [b, s, 4]          (float32)\n          -> comb   [b, s, 4, 4]       (float32, input HC first)\n\n    ``hc_fn`` consumes the RMS-normalized flattened residual but the resulting\n    ``pre`` weights reduce the original, unnormalized residual streams.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    if residual.ndim != 4:\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"residual must have shape [b, s, hc, hidden], got {tuple(residual.shape)}\"\n        )\n    _require_floating(\"residual\", residual)\n    _require_floating(\"hc_fn\", hc_fn)\n    _validate_hyperparameters(\n        norm_eps=norm_eps, sinkhorn_iters=sinkhorn_iters, hc_eps=hc_eps\n    )\n    batch, sequence, hc_mult, hidden_size = residual.shape\n    if batch < 1 or sequence < 1 or hc_mult < 1 or hidden_size < 1:\n        raise ValueError(\"residual dimensions must all be positive\")\n\n    mix_features = (2 + hc_mult) * hc_mult\n    flattened_hidden = hc_mult * hidden_size\n    if tuple(hc_fn.shape) != (mix_features, flattened_hidden):\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"hc_fn shape {tuple(hc_fn.shape)} != \"\n            f\"({mix_features}, {flattened_hidden})\"\n        )\n    if residual.device != hc_fn.device:\n        raise ValueError(\"residual and hc_fn must be on the same device\")\n\n    flattened = residual.flatten(2).float()\n    inverse_rms = torch.rsqrt(\n        flattened.square().mean(dim=-1, keepdim=True) + norm_eps\n    )\n    mixes = F.linear(flattened, hc_fn.float()) * inverse_rms\n    pre, post, comb = hc_split_sinkhorn(\n        mixes,\n        hc_scale,\n        hc_base,\n        hc_mult=hc_mult,\n        sinkhorn_iters=sinkhorn_iters,\n        eps=hc_eps,\n    )\n    hidden = torch.einsum(\"bsh,bshd->bsd\", pre, residual.float())\n    return hidden.to(residual.dtype), post, comb\n\n\ndef hc_post(\n    branch_output: torch.Tensor,\n    residual: torch.Tensor,\n    post: torch.Tensor,\n    comb: torch.Tensor,\n) -> torch.Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Expand one branch output and update the HC residual streams.\n\n    ``branch_output`` is ``[b, s, hidden]`` and ``residual`` is\n    ``[b, s, hc, hidden]``.  ``comb[k, j]`` moves input stream ``k`` into output\n    stream ``j``; therefore the efficient contraction is ``comb.T @ residual``.\n    The returned ``[b, s, hc, hidden]`` tensor has ``branch_output.dtype``.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    if branch_output.ndim != 3:\n        raise ValueError(\n            \"branch_output must have shape [b, s, hidden], got \"\n            f\"{tuple(branch_output.shape)}\"\n        )\n    if residual.ndim != 4:\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"residual must have shape [b, s, hc, hidden], got {tuple(residual.shape)}\"\n        )\n    _require_floating(\"branch_output\", branch_output)\n    _require_floating(\"residual\", residual)\n    _require_floating(\"post\", post)\n    _require_floating(\"comb\", comb)\n\n    batch, sequence, hc_mult, hidden_size = residual.shape\n    if tuple(branch_output.shape) != (batch, sequence, hidden_size):\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"branch_output shape {tuple(branch_output.shape)} != \"\n            f\"({batch}, {sequence}, {hidden_size})\"\n        )\n    if tuple(post.shape) != (batch, sequence, hc_mult):\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"post shape {tuple(post.shape)} != ({batch}, {sequence}, {hc_mult})\"\n        )\n    if tuple(comb.shape) != (batch, sequence, hc_mult, hc_mult):\n        raise ValueError(\n            f\"comb shape {tuple(comb.shape)} != \"\n            f\"({batch}, {sequence}, {hc_mult}, {hc_mult})\"\n        )\n    devices = {branch_output.device, residual.device, post.device, comb.device}\n    if len(devices) != 1:\n        raise ValueError(\"branch_output, residual, post, and comb must share a device\")\n\n    residual_mix = torch.matmul(comb.float().transpose(-1, -2), residual.float())\n    branch_mix = post.float().unsqueeze(-1) * branch_output.float().unsqueeze(-2)\n    return (branch_mix + {"parentUuid":"b98aee34-8bd9-4951-8ad1-23b29cdc8720","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"25d32680-091b-497c-9be8-0fc1785d196f","agentId":"a2fac59ece98737ad","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01JLGZ4W69ojZxSJdVdiQ4Fr","type":"tool_result","content":"===moe_forward.py gate 55-162===\ndef gate_forward_with_boundary(\n    x: torch.Tensor,\n    weight: torch.Tensor,\n    bias: torch.Tensor,\n    *,\n    topk: int = 6,\n    route_scale: float = 2.5,\n) -> GateForwardTensors:\n    \"\"\"Run the learned sqrt-softplus gate used from layer 3 onward.\n\n    Bias changes expert selection only. Routing weights come from the unbiased\n    scores, are normalized per row, and are then multiplied by ``route_scale``.\n    The returned margin is the biased k-th score minus the (k+1)-th score for\n    every row; a small margin identifies routing decisions sensitive to noise.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    if x.ndim != 2 or weight.ndim != 2 or bias.ndim != 1:\n        raise ValueError(\"x/weight/bias must have ranks 2/2/1\")\n    experts, hidden = weight.shape\n    if x.shape[1] != hidden:\n        raise ValueError(f\"x hidden size {x.shape[1]} != gate hidden size {hidden}\")\n    if bias.numel() != experts:\n        raise ValueError(f\"gate bias size {bias.numel()} != experts {experts}\")\n    if not isinstance(topk, int) or isinstance(topk, bool) or not 0 < topk < experts:\n        raise ValueError(\"topk must be a positive integer smaller than expert count\")\n    if not math.isfinite(route_scale) or route_scale <= 0:\n        raise ValueError(\"route_scale must be finite and positive\")\n\n    scores = F.softplus(F.linear(x.float(), weight.float())).sqrt()\n    selection_scores = scores + bias.float()\n    selected_values, selected_ids = selection_scores.topk(topk + 1, dim=-1)\n    ids = selected_ids[:, :topk]\n    margin = selected_values[:, topk - 1] - selected_values[:, topk]\n    routing_weights = scores.gather(1, ids)\n    routing_weights = routing_weights / routing_weights.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\n    routing_weights = routing_weights * float(route_scale)\n    return GateForwardTensors(\n        routing_weights=routing_weights.float(),\n        routing_ids=ids.to(torch.int32),\n        margin=margin.float(),\n        selection_ids=selected_ids,\n        selection_scores=selected_values.float(),\n    )\n\n\ndef gate_forward(\n    x: torch.Tensor,\n    weight: torch.Tensor,\n    bias: torch.Tensor,\n    *,\n    topk: int = 6,\n    route_scale: float = 2.5,\n) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:\n    result = gate_forward_with_boundary(\n        x,\n        weight,\n        bias,\n        topk=topk,\n        route_scale=route_scale,\n    )\n    return result.routing_weights, result.routing_ids, result.margin\n\n\ndef hash_gate_forward(\n    x: torch.Tensor,\n    weight: torch.Tensor,\n    tid2eid: torch.Tensor,\n    input_ids: torch.Tensor,\n    *,\n    route_scale: float = 2.5,\n) -> HashGateForwardTensors:\n    \"\"\"Run the first-three-layer token-ID router without a learned top-k.\n\n    Hash layers still compute sqrt-softplus expert scores for route weights.\n    Only the selected expert IDs come from the checkpoint ``tid2eid`` table.\n    Keeping the table lookup and score gather explicit prevents synthetic expert\n    IDs from silently entering the real layer-2 path.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    if x.ndim != 2 or weight.ndim != 2 or tid2eid.ndim != 2:\n        raise ValueError(\"x/weight/tid2eid must have ranks 2/2/2\")\n    experts, hidden = weight.shape\n    if x.shape[1] != hidden:\n        raise ValueError(f\"x hidden size {x.shape[1]} != gate hidden size {hidden}\")\n    if input_ids.ndim != 1 or input_ids.shape[0] != x.shape[0]:\n        raise ValueError(\"input_ids must contain one token ID per gate row\")\n    if input_ids.dtype != torch.int64 or tid2eid.dtype != torch.int64:\n        raise TypeError(\"hash input IDs and tid2eid must be int64\")\n    if tid2eid.shape[1] <= 0 or tid2eid.shape[1] >= experts:\n        raise ValueError(\"tid2eid top-k width must be positive and smaller than experts\")\n    if x.device != weight.device or x.device != tid2eid.device:\n        raise ValueError(\"hash gate tensors must share one device\")\n    if input_ids.device != x.device:\n        raise ValueError(\"hash gate input IDs must share the 55-162===\ndef gate_forward_with_boundary(\n    x: torch.Tensor,\n    weight: torch.Tensor,\n    bias: torch.Tensor,\n    *,\n    topk: int = 6,\n    route_scale: float = 2.5,\n) -> GateForwardTensors:\n    \"\"\"Run the learned sqrt-softplus gate used from layer 3 onward.\n\n    Bias changes expert selection only. Routing weights come from the unbiased\n    scores, are normalized per row, and are then multiplied by ``route_scale``.\n    The returned margin is the biased k-th score minus the (k+1)-th score for\n    every row; a small margin identifies routing decisions sensitive to noise.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    if x.ndim != 2 or weight.ndim != 2 or bias.ndim != 1:\n        raise ValueError(\"x/weight/bias must have ranks 2/2/1\")\n    experts, hidden = weight.shape\n    if x.shape[1] != hidden:\n        raise ValueError(f\"x hidden size {x.shape[1]} != gate hidden size {hidden}\")\n    if bias.numel() != experts:\n        raise ValueError(f\"gate bias size {bias.numel()} != experts {experts}\")\n    if not isinstance(topk, int) or isinstance(topk, bool) or not 0 < topk < experts:\n        raise ValueError(\"topk must be a positive integer smaller than expert count\")\n    if not math.isfinite(route_scale) or route_scale <= 0:\n        raise ValueError(\"route_scale must be finite and positive\")\n\n    scores = F.softplus(F.linear(x.float(), weight.float())).sqrt()\n    selection_scores = scores + bias.float()\n    selected_values, selected_ids = selection_scores.topk(topk + 1, dim=-1)\n    ids = selected_ids[:, :topk]\n    margin = selected_values[:, topk - 1] - selected_values[:, topk]\n    routing_weights = scores.gather(1, ids)\n    routing_weights = routing_weights / routing_weights.sum(dim=-1, keepdim=True)\n    routing_weights = routing_weights * float(route_scale)\n    return GateForwardTensors(\n        routing_weights=routing_weights.float(),\n        routing_ids=ids.to(torch.int32),\n        margin=margin.float(),\n        selection_ids=selected_ids,\n        selection_scores=selected_values.float(),\n    )\n\n\ndef gate_forward(\n    x: torch.Tensor,\n    weight: torch.Tensor,\n    bias: torch.Tensor,\n    *,\n    topk: int = 6,\n    route_scale: float = 2.5,\n) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:\n    result = gate_forward_with_boundary(\n        x,\n        weight,\n        bias,\n        topk=topk,\n        route_scale=route_scale,\n    )\n    return result.routing_weights, result.routing_ids, path.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    if x.ndim != 2 or weight.ndim != 2 or tid2eid.ndim != 2:\n        raise ValueError(\"x/weight/tid2eid must have ranks 2/2/2\")\n    experts, hidden = weight.shape\n    if x.shape[1] != hidden:\n        raise ValueError(f\"x hidden size {x.shape[1]} != gate hidden size {hidden}\")\n    if input_ids.ndim != 1 or input_ids.shape[0] != x.shape[0]:\n        raise :1224-1233(`forward_stateful_decode_tensor`)、:1373-1380(`forward_decode_tensor`)、:1553-1560(`__call__`)。模式均为 `wo_a.reshape(o_groups, o_rank, num_heads*head_dim//o_groups)` + `einsum(\"bsgd,grd->bsgr\", grouped, wo_a)`。这三处用 `cfg.o_groups`,是**参数化的**,只要 config.validate 放行即可,无需改 einsum 本体。\n\n---\n\n## 3. moe_runtime.py\n\n- **fused_marlin_moe 调用点**:import `_fused_marlin_moe`
